Shopping daama (or *shoppi daama*) koyima (or *koyimaa*) to buy galbeen (or *galbeena*) jima (or *jimaa*) na tax na excises a certain locations. **Note:** This is a possible translation, and variations might exist depending on the specific region and dialect of Fulfulde in Nigeria. I've provided a few options for words to reflect the richness of the language. I prioritized clarity and common usage. The use of "daama" or "shoppi daama" is common for "duty-free shopping."
